17th-64th place finishers
=========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 4, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











You've seen the [Top 8](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpmad16/top-8-decklists-2016-12-04) and the [Top 16](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpmad16/9th-16-decklists-2016-12-04). But prize money went down to 64th place. Below, you can find the decklists of the players who finished in 17th-64th place.


**Decklists of players with 36 match points (12-3)**
